                is: function() {

                        eqUrls = this.eqUrls,
                        nowUrl = location.href;

                    for (var i = 0,ln = urls.length; i < ln; i++) {
                        if (nowUrl.indexOf(urls[i]) != -1) {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }

                    for (var i = 0,ln = eqUrls.length; i < ln; i++) {
                        if (nowUrl === eqUrls[i]) {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }

                    return false;
                }
            },

                {
                    name: 'def',
                    css: ['https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/L3/material/css5/uniqlo.css', 'https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/css/top.css'],

            initUQ: function() {

                var rules = this.rules;
                for (var i = 0, ln = rules.length; i < ln; i++) {
                    if (rules[i].is()) {
                        writeCSS(rules[i].css)
                        writeJS(rules[i].js);
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        var writeJS = function(args) {
            var arr = [];
            for (var i = 0, ln = args.length; i < ln; i++) {
                arr.push('<');
                arr.push('script src="' + args[i] + '"');
                arr.push('>');
                arr.push('</');
                arr.push('script');
                arr.push('>');
            }
            if (arr.length > 0) {
                document.write(arr.join(''));
            }
        }

        var writeCSS = function(args) {
            var arr = [];
            for (var i = 0, ln = args.length; i < ln; i++) {
                arr.push('<');
                arr.push('link href="' + args[i] + '" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="all" /');
                arr.push('>');
            }
            if (arr.length > 0) {
                document.write(arr.join(''));
            }
        }

        importFile.initUQ();

    })();

        /////json锟斤拷锟斤拷///// 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟剿碉拷锟斤拷锟揭憋拷图片锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
        var jsonMod = '{ "mod" : [' +
                '{ "name":"women","href":"https://uniqlo.tmall.com/p/rd103866.htm","img":"https://img.alicdn.com/imgextra/i2/196993935/TB2HjtZjFXXXXbVXpXXXXXXXXXX-196993935.jpg"},' +
                '{ "name":"men","href":"https://uniqlo.tmall.com/p/rd103866.htm","img":"https://img.alicdn.com/imgextra/i2/196993935/TB2Jx1ejFXXXXceXXXXXXXXXXXX-196993935.jpg"},' +
                '{ "name":"kids","href":"http://www.uniqlo.cn/search.htm?spm=0.0.0.0.GY6T4J&search=y&scid=1176015736&queryType=cat&scname=MdTCMTHI1cnPvNzQwsa3","img":"https://img.alicdn.com/imgextra/i3/196993935/TB2n2R5jFXXXXaGXpXXXXXXXXXX-196993935.jpg"},' +
                '{ "name":"baby","href":"http://www.uniqlo.cn/search.htm?spm=0.0.0.0.OeTLRc&search=y&scid=237719246&queryType=cat&scname=1%2B7QwsnPvNzJzMa3IEJBQlk%3D","img":"https://img.alicdn.com/imgextra/i1/196993935/TB2n83yjFXXXXXtXpXXXXXXXXXX-196993935.jpg"} ]}';

        /////
        $('div.navBox div.mod').each(function(a, b) {
            var myJson = eval('(' + jsonMod + ')'), //锟斤拷锟斤拷
                    newObjA = $('<a>'),
                    newObjImg = $('<img>'),
                    img_src = myJson.mod[a].img,
                    a_href = myJson.mod[a].href;
            $(b).html(newObjA);
            $(b).find('a').html(newObjImg);
            newObjA.attr('href', a_href);
            newObjImg.attr('src', img_src);
        });
        /////////////////
        $('img.overimg').each(function(img_l, img_ob) {
            var img_lk = $(img_ob).attr('src'),
                    img_w = $(img_ob).attr('width'),
                    img_h = $(img_ob).attr('height');
            $(img_ob).parent().parent().css({
                'height': img_h / 2,
                //'width': img_w,
                'background-image': 'url(' + img_lk + ')'
            });
            $(img_ob).attr('src', 'https://img.alicdn.com/imgextra/i4/196993935/T2n1NyXIpXXXXXXXXX_!!196993935.gif');
            //
            $(img_ob).click(function() {
                if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE") > 0) { //锟斤拷锟斤拷IEBUG
                    $('img.overimg').removeAttr('id').parent().parent().css('background-position-y', 0);
                    $('img.overimg').removeAttr('id').parent().parent().css('background-position-x', 'center');
                    $(this).attr('id', 'down').parent().parent().css('background-position-y', img_h / 2);
                } else {
                    $('img.overimg').removeAttr('id').parent().parent().css('background-position', 'top');
                    $(this).attr('id', 'down').parent().parent().css('background-position', 'bottom');
                }
            });
            //
            $(img_ob).hover(function() {
                var id_Name = $(this).attr('id')
                if (id_Name != 'down') {
                    if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE") > 0) { //锟斤拷锟斤拷IEBUG
                        $(this).parent().parent().css('background-position-y', img_h / 2);
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent().parent().css('background-position', 'bottom');
                    }
                };
            }, function() {
                var id_Name = $(this).attr('id')
                if (id_Name != 'down') {
                    if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE") > 0) {
                        $(this).parent().parent().css('background-position-y', 0);
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent().parent().css('background-position', 'top');
                    }
                };
            });
        });

<script type="text/javascript">
    //锟斤拷锟斤拷锟剿碉拷锟斤拷头锟斤拷锟揭边关闭帮拷钮
    ratio = 0.92;
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var n = $(window).width();
        $(".navBox").width(n * ratio);
        $(".navBox .add").each(function() {
            var arrow = $(this).find(".arrow");
            var cross = $(this).find(".cross");
            var target = $("#" + arrow.attr("data-align"));
            $(this).css({
                //"margin-left": left
            }).attr("data-w", target.width()).attr("data-name", arrow.attr("data-align"));
        });
    });
</script>
<script type="text/javascript" defer>
    /**
     * UNIQLO L1 Scripts
     *
     * @author    katsuma@team-lab.com
     * @version    1.0
     * @require    jquery 1.6
     * @require    jquery easing 1.3
     */
    /*
     * uniqlo utils
     */
    $.extend({
        debug: location.href.indexOf("file:///") == 0,
        log: function(msg) {
            if ($.debug && window.console) console.log(msg);
        }
    });

    /*
     * image rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["rollover"] = function(options) {
            var settings = $.extend({
                suffix: "_o"
            }, options);
            var _imgs = [];
            this.each(function() {
                var dsrc = $(this).attr("src");
                var ftype = dsrc.substring(dsrc.lastIndexOf("."), dsrc.length);
                var hsrc = dsrc.indexOf(settings.suffix + ftype) > 0 ? dsrc : dsrc.replace(ftype, settings.suffix + ftype);
                // preload
                _imgs.push(new Image());
                _imgs[_imgs.length - 1].src = hsrc;
                $(this).attr({
                    dsrc: dsrc,
                    hsrc: hsrc
                }).mouseover(function() {
                    $(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("hsrc"));
                }).mouseout(function() {
                    $(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("dsrc"));
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * image rollover toggle plugin
     * @require image rollover plugin
     */

    (function($) {
        $.fn["rolloverToggle"] = function(options) {
            var settings = $.extend({
                current: true,
                suffix: "_o"
            }, options);
            this.each(function() {
                if (settings.current) {

                    // default -> hover
                    $(this).attr({
                        dsrc: $(this).attr("hsrc"),
                        src: $(this).attr("hsrc")
                    });
                } else {}
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * image loader with callback plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["imageLoader"] = function(callback) {
            var _length = $(this).length;
            var _loaded = function() {
                _length--;
                if (_length == 0) callback.apply();
            };
            this.each(function() {
                $("<img>").attr("src", $(this).attr("src")).load(_loaded).error(_loaded);
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * uniqlo header plugin
     * @require image rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["header"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                imgClass: ".imgover",
                mainID: ".id_navHeader",
                subClass: "navCategory",
                cartID: ".id_gnav_cart_trigger",
                searchID: ".id_searchFocus",
                duration: 200,
                animate: false
            }, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                // 锟截ッワ拷锟节讹拷锟紸锟接わ拷锟絯锟狡わ拷锟绞わ拷锟轿はワ拷锟斤拷锟矫ワ拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                $(this).find("a").focus(function() {
                    $(this).blur();
                });
                $(this).find("ul.navCategory>li>a").click(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr("href") == "#") return false;
                });
                var _timer_header_toggle;
                $(".id_navHeader").hover(function() {
                    clearTimeout(_timer_header_toggle);
                    $(".id_header").stop().animate({
                        height: 100
                    }, 400, "easeOutQuint", function() {
                        $(".id_header").css({
                            overflow: "visible"
                        });
                    });
                }, function() {});
                $(this).find(">.navArea").hover(function() {}, function() {
                    _timer_header_toggle = setTimeout(function() {
                        $(".id_header").stop().delay(100).animate({
                            height: 50
                        }, 400, "easeOutQuint", function() {
                            $(".id_header").css({
                                overflow: "hidden"
                            });
                        });
                    }, 500);






                });
                // 锟节讹拷锟紸锟接わ拷锟絎锟接ワ拷锟斤拷锟絗锟斤拷锟矫ワ拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟饺憋拷示锟斤拷锟斤拷
                $(".id_navHeader>li").mouseover(function() {
                    $(".id_navHeader>li").removeClass("current");
                    $(this).addClass("current");
                });
                // 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟秸ワ拷锟絗锟斤拷
                $(this).find(settings.searchID).focus(function() {
                    $(this).parent().parent().addClass("inputFocus");
                }).blur(function() {
                    $(this).parent().parent().removeClass("inputFocus");
                });
                // 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟窖ニー锟叫讹拷
                if ($("body.id_company").length > 0) {
                    $(".id_header_company").parent().addClass("focus").end().find(">img").rolloverToggle().end().siblings("ul").removeClass("navCategoryHidden");
                }
                // 锟斤拷锟紸锟接ドワ拷锟矫プワ拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                $(settings.mainID).find("li").hover(function() {
                    if (!settings.animate && $(this).parent().hasClass(settings.mainID.replace(".", ""))) {
                        $(this).find(">ul").show();
                    } else {
                        $(this).find(">ul:not(:animated)").slideDown(settings.duration);
                    }
                }, function() {
                    // 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟饺ワ拷锟狡ワ拷锟斤拷锟节讹拷锟紸锟接わ拷锟絔锟斤拷锟绞わ拷

                    if ($(this).find(">ul").hasClass(settings.subClass)) return;
                    if (!settings.animate && $(this).parent().hasClass(settings.mainID.replace(".", ""))) {
                        $(this).find(".sub").hide().end().find(">ul").hide();
                    } else {
                        $(this).find(">ul").slideUp(settings.duration, function() {
                            // 锟斤拷锟剿ワ拷锟絗锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟轿ワ拷锟斤拷锟竭ング次第で碉拷锟斤拷锟紸锟接わ拷取锟斤拷锟叫わ拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟轿で忥拷锟狡的わ拷锟絔锟斤拷锟斤拷
                            $(this).find(".sub").hide();
                        });
                    }
                });
                // 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟矫ピングワ拷锟絗锟斤拷
                if (settings.animate) {
                    $(settings.cartID).parent().hover(function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul:not(:animated)").slideDown(settings.duration);
                    }, function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").slideUp(settings.duration);
                    });
                } else {
                    $(settings.cartID).parent().hover(function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").show();
                    }, function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").hide();
                    });
                }
                // 锟斤拷锟絗锟诫オ锟絗锟叫ー锟斤拷锟斤拷
                $(this).find(settings.imgClass).unbind("mouseover").unbind("mouseout").parent().parent().hover(function() {
                    var $img = $(this).find(">a>img");
                    $img.attr("src", $img.attr("hsrc"));
                }, function() {
                    var $img = $(this).find(">a>img");
                    $img.attr("src", $img.attr("dsrc"));
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);


    /*
     * L1 animated rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["animatedRollover"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                duration: 350
            }, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                $(this).hover(function() {
                    $(this).find(".overlay").stop().css({
                        left: -690
                    }).animate({
                        left: -230
                    }, settings.duration, "easeOutQuart");
                }, function() {
                    $(this).find(".overlay").stop().animate({
                        left: 230
                    }, settings.duration * .6, "easeInCubic");
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * L1 uniqlo logo allocation plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["logoAllocation"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                // settings no logo
                cofMin: 400,
                cofMax: 600,
                retryMax: 10
            }, options);
            var _content_logo_allocations = [];
            var _content_logo_element = $("<li />").addClass("logo_block").addClass("contentH10").css({






























                display: "none"
            });
            // main
            this.each(function(i, elem) {
                // 4-6锟街ワ拷锟矫ワ拷锟斤拷锟饺にワ拷锟斤拷1锟斤拷
                var cof = Math.floor(Math.random() * (settings.cofMax - settings.cofMin + 1)) + settings.cofMin;
                var len = $(this).find(">li").length;
                var cnt = Math.floor(len / cof);
                for (var j = 0; j < cnt; j++) {
                    var k, h, r = settings.retryMax;
                    while (true) {
                        k = cof * j + j + 1;
                        k += Math.floor(Math.random() * cof) + 1;
                        // 锟斤拷锟斤拷锟角ッワ拷锟斤拷锟津グワ拷锟矫ド凤拷锟脚に凤拷锟経
                        h = 0;
                        $(this).find(">li").each(function(i, elem) {
                            h += $(this).hasClass("contentH05") ? 0 : $(this).hasClass("contentH10") ? 1 : 2;
                            if (k == i + 1) {
                                h++;
                                return false;
                            }
                        });
                        // 锟斤拷锟終锟接になわ拷锟绞わ拷锟借う锟剿ワ拷锟街ワ拷锟絫锟斤拷锟斤拷锟叫讹拷
                        if ($.inArray(h, _content_logo_allocations) != -1) {
                            $.log("锟斤拷锟街っわ拷锟絗: " + i.toString() + "-" + j.toString());
                            r--;
                            if (r > 0) continue;
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                    if (r > 0) {
                        _content_logo_allocations.push(h);
                        $(this).find(">li:nth-child(" + k.toString() + ")").after(_content_logo_element.clone());
                    }
                }
            });
            if ($(".id_top").hasClass("selected")) {
                // ie fix
                if (!$.support.opacity) {
                    $(".id_content_blocks .logo_block").show();
                } else {
                    $(".id_content_blocks .logo_block").slideDown(600, "easeOutQuint");
                }
            }
            $.log(_content_logo_allocations);
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * L1 image crossfade plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["crossFade"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                selector: ">a>img:odd",
                duration: 400,
                //"interval" : 1330
                interval: 2666
            }, options);
            // ie fix
            if (!$.support.opacity) settings.interval *= 1.5;
            // main
            var $target = $(this).filter(":visible").find(settings.selector);
            var _timer = setInterval(function() {
                $target.stop(true, true).fadeToggle(settings.duration, "easeInOutQuart");
            }, settings.interval);
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * animated page top plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["animatedPageTop"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({}, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                $(this).click(function() {
                    //$(window).scrollTop(0);
                    $("html,body").animate({
                        scrollTop: 0
                    }, "slow", "easeOutQuart");
                    $(this).blur();
                    return false;
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    (function($) {
        // initialize
        $(function() {
            $(".imgover").rollover();
            $(".id_header").header();
            // lazy evaluation
            setTimeout(function() {
                $(".id_content_blocks>ul").logoAllocation();
                $(".id_content_blocks>ul>li").animatedRollover();
                $(".id_content_blocks .contentCrossFade").crossFade();
                $(".id_goPageTop>a").animatedPageTop();
            }, 600);
        });

    })(jQuery);
</script>

<script>
    var n = $(window).width();
    $(".box_boss").width(n).css({
        marginLeft: -n * 0.5
    });
    $(".box_show ul li img").width(n * ratio);
    var z = $(".box_subnav ul li").width();
    $(".box_subnav ul li").find("img").width(z);
    $(".box_subnav li").first().find(".current_img").show().css({
        marginTop: -10
    });
    var x = 0;
    $(".box_subnav ul li").click(function() {
        x = $(this).index();

        $(".box_run").stop().animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);

        $(this).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });
    $(".left_btn").click(function() {
        if (0 < x) {
            x = x - 1
        } else {
            x = $(".box_show ul li").length - 1
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });
    $(".right_btn").click(function() {
        if (x < $(".box_show ul li").length - 1) {
            x = x + 1
        } else {
            x = 0
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500)
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });


    function run() {
        $(".box_run").stop(true, true);
        $(".current_img").stop(true, true);

        if (x < $(".box_show ul li").length - 1) {
            x = x + 1
        } else {
            x = 0
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    };
    /*setInterval(run,3000);*/
    t = setInterval(run, 3000);
    $(".box_show,.box_subnav ul li").mouseenter(function() {
        clearInterval(t)
    }).mouseleave(function() {
        //setInterval(run,3000)
        t = setInterval(run, 3000);
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var speed = 5e3;
        //锟皆讹拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟劫讹拷
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", 1);
        //锟斤拷始锟斤拷锟斤拷值
        /*锟揭硷拷头*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").hover(function() {
            $(this).css({
                "background-position":"left bottom"
            });
        }, function() {
            $(this).removeAttr("style");
        });
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").click(function() {
            var page = $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data");
            ////
            var li_l = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w * 3;
            $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
            ////
            if (!$(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                //锟叫讹拷图片展示锟斤拷锟斤拷锟角凤拷锟斤拷锟节讹拷锟斤拷锟阶讹拷
                if (page == li_l) {
                    //锟斤拷循锟斤拷
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li:first").clone().attr("id", "cop").appendTo($(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box"));
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                        width:ul_w + li_w + "px"
                    });
                    //锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            left:0
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            width:ul_w + "px"
                        });
                    });
                    page = 1;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                } else {
                    //锟斤拷锟斤拷
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    });
                    page++;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                }
            }
        });
        /*锟揭硷拷头锟斤拷锟斤拷*/
        /*锟斤拷锟斤拷头*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").hover(function() {
            $(this).css({
                "background-position":"left bottom"
            });
        }, function() {
            $(this).removeAttr("style");
        });
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").click(function() {
            var page = $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data");
            ////
            var li_l = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w;
            $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
            ////
            if (!$(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                if (page == 1) {
                    //锟斤拷循锟斤拷
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li:last").clone().attr("id", "cop").prependTo($(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box"));
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                        width:ul_w + li_w + "px",
                        left:-li_w
                    });
                    //锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟饺硷拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"+=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            left:-(li_w * (page - 1))
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            width:ul_w + "px"
                        });
                    });
                    page = li_l;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                } else {
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"+=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    });
                    page--;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                }
            }
        });
        /*锟斤拷锟斤拷头锟斤拷锟斤拷*/
        /*锟斤拷锟斤拷图*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.btn").each(function(i, n) {
            var a = $(n).width();
            var b = $(n).parent().width();
            /*$(n).css({left:(b/2)-(a/2)})*/
            $(n).find("div").each(function(j, m) {
                //锟街憋拷筛选锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                $(m).eq(j).css({
                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                });
                $(m).hover(function() {
                    if (!$(this).hasClass("this") && $(this).hasClass("bo")) {
                        $(this).css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                    }
                }, function() {
                    if (!$(this).hasClass("this")) {
                        $(this).removeAttr("style");
                    }
                });
                ////
                var li_l = $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w;
                $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
                ////
                $(m).mouseenter(function() {
                    $(this).addClass("this").css({
                        "background-position":"left bottom"
                    }).mouseleave(function() {
                        $(this).stop();
                    });
                    $(this).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-" + li_w * j
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart");
                    page = j + 1;
                    //匹锟斤拷锟斤拷锟揭硷拷头
                    $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                });
            });
        });
        /*锟斤拷锟皆斤拷锟斤拷*/
        /*锟皆讹拷锟街诧拷*/
        var boxliw = $(".big_box_04 .show_view").width();
        $("div.big_box_04").each(function(l, o) {
            var div_h = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box li img").height();
            var span_h = $(o).find("div.btn div").height();
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li").css("width", boxliw + "px");
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li img").css("width", boxliw + "px");
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li img").css("height", "auto");
            /*$(o).css({height:div_h+span_h});
             $(o).find('div.show_view').css({height:div_h});*/
            var handle;
            function start_slide() {
                var page = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data");
                ////
                var li_l = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = boxliw, ul_w = li_l * li_w;
                $(o).find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
                ////
                handle = setInterval(function() {
                    if (!$(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                        //锟叫讹拷图片展示锟斤拷锟斤拷锟角凤拷锟斤拷锟节讹拷锟斤拷锟阶讹拷
                        if (page == li_l) {
                            //锟斤拷循锟斤拷
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").find("li:first").clone().attr("id", "cop").appendTo($(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box"));
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").css({
                                width:ul_w + li_w + "px"
                            });
                            //锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷锟斤拷
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").animate({
                                left:"-=" + li_w
                            }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                                $(this).css({
                                    left:0
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                                $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                                $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").css({
                                    width:ul_w + "px"
                                });
                            });
                            page = 1;
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                        } else {
                            //锟斤拷锟斤拷
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").animate({
                                left:"-=" + li_w
                            }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                            });
                            page++;
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                        }
                    }
                }, speed);
            }
            ///
            function stop_slide() {
                clearInterval(handle);
            }
            //////
            setTimeout(function() {
                start_slide();
            }, 0);
            //锟斤拷锟斤拷IEbug
            $(o).hover(function() {
                //锟皆讹拷锟斤拷始
                stop_slide();
            }, function() {
                start_slide();
            });
        });
    });

    $(window).bind("load", function() {
        //锟接迟硷拷锟斤拷
        var timeout = setTimeout(function() {
            $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view ul.banner_box li").removeAttr("style");
            $("div.big_box_04").find("img").trigger("sporty");
        }, 400);
    });

    $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").hide();

    $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").hide();

    $("div.big_box_04.show_view").mouseenter(function() {
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").show();
        $("div.big_box_04.left").show();
    });

    $("div.big_box_04.show_view").mouseleave(function() {
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").hide();
        $("div.big_box_04.left").hide();
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
        var categoryPage = false;
        $('.id_navHeader>li>a[class^="id_header_"]').click(function () {
            categoryPage = true;
            var target = $(this).attr('href').substr(2);
            $("div.navSubSectionHeader").hide();
            $("div.navPlaceholder").hide();
            $("div.navPlaceholder_" + target).show();
            $('div.navSubSectionHeader_' + target).show();
        });
        $("area.navSectionHeader").click(function () {
            if (categoryPage) {
                var ref = $(this).attr('data-ref');
                $(".id_navHeader>li>a[href='" + ref + "']").trigger('click');
                return false;
            }
        });
        $("a.id_top").click(function () {
            categoryPage = false;
            $("div.navSubSectionHeader").show();
            $("div.navPlaceholder").show();
        });
    });
</script>

		(function() {
			var S = KISSY, DOM = S.DOM,
				loginPlace = DOM.get('#J_ExteralLoginPlace');
			if (loginPlace) {
				var params = S.unparam(DOM.attr(S.get('#J_ExternalShopParams'), 'data-info-value'));
				if (params) {
					var lg = S.Cookie.get('_l_g_'),
						nk = S.Cookie.get('_nk_'),
						lg2 = S.Cookie.get('lg'),
						nk2 = S.Cookie.get('nk');
					function getHan(str) {
						var myReg = /\\u(.{4,4})/g;
						if(!myReg.test(str)){
							return str.replace(/"/g,'');
						}else{
							return str.replace(/\\u(.{4,4})/g, function(m, s) {
								 return String.fromCharCode(parseInt(s, 16));
							});
						}
					}
								//锟斤拷录锟矫伙拷
					if (!!( lg && nk )) {

<script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var importFile = {

            rules: [{
                name: 'index',
                urls: ['http://uniqlo.tmall.com', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/p/', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/index.htm', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/#', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/?', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/shop/view_shop.htm', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/shop/viewShop.htm', 'prt=1319799519134', 'view_page-155260302.htm', 'prt=1319799750758', 'prt=1319799818045', '1319799901234', 'previewSuperShop.htm?pageId=155260302', 'previewSuperShop.htm?pageId=155203461', 'design.htm?pageId=155203461', 'view_page-155203461.htm', 'view_page-676316647.htm', 'view_page-676317047.htm'],
                eqUrls: ['http://uniqlo.taobao.com/', 'http://uniqlo.tmall.com/', 'http://www.uniqlo.cn/'],
                css: ['https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/L1_990/css/uniqlo.css',
                    'https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/css/top.css'
                ],
                js: ['https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/js/lib.js', 'https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/js/L1_nav_20150702.js'],

                is: function() {
                    var urls = this.urls,
                        eqUrls = this.eqUrls,
                        nowUrl = location.href;

                    for (var i = 0,ln = urls.length; i < ln; i++) {
                        if (nowUrl.indexOf(urls[i]) != -1) {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }

                    for (var i = 0,ln = eqUrls.length; i < ln; i++) {
                        if (nowUrl === eqUrls[i]) {
                            return true;
                        }
                    }

                    return false;
                }
            },

                {
                    name: 'def',
                    css: ['https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/L3/material/css5/uniqlo.css', 'https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/css/top.css'],
                    js: ['https://uniqlo.image.alimmdn.com/L1/siterenew/js/lib.js'],

                    is: function() {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            ],


            initUQ: function() {

                var rules = this.rules;
                for (var i = 0, ln = rules.length; i < ln; i++) {
                    if (rules[i].is()) {
                        writeCSS(rules[i].css)
                        writeJS(rules[i].js);
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        var writeJS = function(args) {
            var arr = [];
            for (var i = 0, ln = args.length; i < ln; i++) {
                arr.push('<');
                arr.push('script src="' + args[i] + '"');
                arr.push('>');
                arr.push('</');
                arr.push('script');
                arr.push('>');
            }
            if (arr.length > 0) {
                document.write(arr.join(''));
            }
        }

        var writeCSS = function(args) {
            var arr = [];
            for (var i = 0, ln = args.length; i < ln; i++) {
                arr.push('<');
                arr.push('link href="' + args[i] + '" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" media="all" /');
                arr.push('>');
            }
            if (arr.length > 0) {
                document.write(arr.join(''));
            }
        }

        importFile.initUQ();

    })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" defer>
    /**
     * UNIQLO L1 Scripts
     *
     * @author    katsuma@team-lab.com
     * @version    1.0
     * @require    jquery 1.6
     * @require    jquery easing 1.3
     */
    /*
     * uniqlo utils
     */
    $.extend({
        debug: location.href.indexOf("file:///") == 0,
        log: function(msg) {
            if ($.debug && window.console) console.log(msg);
        }
    });

    /*
     * image rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["rollover"] = function(options) {
            var settings = $.extend({
                suffix: "_o"
            }, options);
            var _imgs = [];
            this.each(function() {
                var dsrc = $(this).attr("src");
                var ftype = dsrc.substring(dsrc.lastIndexOf("."), dsrc.length);
                var hsrc = dsrc.indexOf(settings.suffix + ftype) > 0 ? dsrc : dsrc.replace(ftype, settings.suffix + ftype);
                // preload
                _imgs.push(new Image());
                _imgs[_imgs.length - 1].src = hsrc;
                $(this).attr({
                    dsrc: dsrc,
                    hsrc: hsrc
                }).mouseover(function() {
                    $(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("hsrc"));
                }).mouseout(function() {
                    $(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("dsrc"));
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * image rollover toggle plugin
     * @require image rollover plugin
     */

    (function($) {
        $.fn["rolloverToggle"] = function(options) {
            var settings = $.extend({
                current: true,
                suffix: "_o"
            }, options);
            this.each(function() {
                if (settings.current) {

                    // default -> hover
                    $(this).attr({
                        dsrc: $(this).attr("hsrc"),
                        src: $(this).attr("hsrc")
                    });
                } else {}
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * image loader with callback plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["imageLoader"] = function(callback) {
            var _length = $(this).length;
            var _loaded = function() {
                _length--;
                if (_length == 0) callback.apply();
            };
            this.each(function() {
                $("<img>").attr("src", $(this).attr("src")).load(_loaded).error(_loaded);
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * uniqlo header plugin
     * @require image rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["header"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                imgClass: ".imgover",
                mainID: ".id_navHeader",
                subClass: "navCategory",
                cartID: ".id_gnav_cart_trigger",
                searchID: ".id_searchFocus",
                duration: 200,
                animate: false
            }, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                // �%������A����w���������������������
                $(this).find("a").focus(function() {
                    $(this).blur();
                });
                $(this).find("ul.navCategory>li>a").click(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr("href") == "#") return false;
                });
                var _timer_header_toggle;
                $(".id_navHeader").hover(function() {
                    clearTimeout(_timer_header_toggle);
                    $(".id_header").stop().animate({
                        height: 100
                    }, 400, "easeOutQuint", function() {
                        $(".id_header").css({
                            overflow: "visible"
                        });
                    });
                }, function() {});
                $(this).find(">.navArea").hover(function() {}, function() {
                    _timer_header_toggle = setTimeout(function() {
                        $(".id_header").stop().delay(100).animate({
                            height: 50
                        }, 400, "easeOutQuint", function() {
                            $(".id_header").css({
                                overflow: "hidden"
                            });
                        });
                    }, 500);






                });
                // ����A����W������`����������1������
                $(".id_navHeader>li").mouseover(function() {
                    $(".id_navHeader>li").removeClass("current");
                    $(this).addClass("current");
                });
                // �����e��`��
                $(this).find(settings.searchID).focus(function() {
                    $(this).parent().parent().addClass("inputFocus");
                }).blur(function() {
                    $(this).parent().parent().removeClass("inputFocus");
                });
                // �����e�`�6�
                if ($("body.id_company").length > 0) {
                    $(".id_header_company").parent().addClass("focus").end().find(">img").rolloverToggle().end().siblings("ul").removeClass("navCategoryHidden");
                }
                // ���A��e���������
                $(settings.mainID).find("li").hover(function() {
                    if (!settings.animate && $(this).parent().hasClass(settings.mainID.replace(".", ""))) {
                        $(this).find(">ul").show();
                    } else {
                        $(this).find(">ul:not(:animated)").slideDown(settings.duration);
                    }
                }, function() {
                    // �������%����������A����]�����

                    if ($(this).find(">ul").hasClass(settings.subClass)) return;
                    if (!settings.animate && $(this).parent().hasClass(settings.mainID.replace(".", ""))) {
                        $(this).find(".sub").hide().end().find(">ul").hide();
                    } else {
                        $(this).find(">ul").slideUp(settings.duration, function() {
                            // ������`�������������W4�������A���!���$�����������$��]����
                            $(this).find(".sub").hide();
                        });
                    }
                });
                // ������%W%��`��
                if (settings.animate) {
                    $(settings.cartID).parent().hover(function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul:not(:animated)").slideDown(settings.duration);
                    }, function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").slideUp(settings.duration);
                    });
                } else {
                    $(settings.cartID).parent().hover(function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").show();
                    }, function() {
                        $(this).find(">ul").hide();
                    });
                }
                // ���`�j�`�)`����
                $(this).find(settings.imgClass).unbind("mouseover").unbind("mouseout").parent().parent().hover(function() {
                    var $img = $(this).find(">a>img");
                    $img.attr("src", $img.attr("hsrc"));
                }, function() {
                    var $img = $(this).find(">a>img");
                    $img.attr("src", $img.attr("dsrc"));
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);


    /*
     * L1 animated rollover plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["animatedRollover"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                duration: 350
            }, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                $(this).hover(function() {
                    $(this).find(".overlay").stop().css({
                        left: -690
                    }).animate({
                        left: -230
                    }, settings.duration, "easeOutQuart");
                }, function() {
                    $(this).find(".overlay").stop().animate({
                        left: 230
                    }, settings.duration * .6, "easeInCubic");
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * L1 uniqlo logo allocation plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["logoAllocation"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                // settings no logo
                cofMin: 400,
                cofMax: 600,
                retryMax: 10
            }, options);
            var _content_logo_allocations = [];
            var _content_logo_element = $("<li />").addClass("logo_block").addClass("contentH10").css({






























                display: "none"
            });
            // main
            this.each(function(i, elem) {
                // 4-6���������$����1��
                var cof = Math.floor(Math.random() * (settings.cofMax - settings.cofMin + 1)) + settings.cofMin;
                var len = $(this).find(">li").length;
                var cnt = Math.floor(len / cof);
                for (var j = 0; j < cnt; j++) {
                    var k, h, r = settings.retryMax;
                    while (true) {
                        k = cof * j + j + 1;
                        k += Math.floor(Math.random() * cof) + 1;
                        // �����������W%���w��d���U
                        h = 0;
                        $(this).find(">li").each(function(i, elem) {
                            h += $(this).hasClass("contentH05") ? 0 : $(this).hasClass("contentH10") ? 1 : 2;
                            if (k == i + 1) {
                                h++;
                                return false;
                            }
                        });
                        // ���K���������&�������t�����6�
                        if ($.inArray(h, _content_logo_allocations) != -1) {
                            $.log("�������`: " + i.toString() + "-" + j.toString());
                            r--;
                            if (r > 0) continue;
                        }
                        break;
                    }
                    if (r > 0) {
                        _content_logo_allocations.push(h);
                        $(this).find(">li:nth-child(" + k.toString() + ")").after(_content_logo_element.clone());
                    }
                }
            });
            if ($(".id_top").hasClass("selected")) {
                // ie fix
                if (!$.support.opacity) {
                    $(".id_content_blocks .logo_block").show();
                } else {
                    $(".id_content_blocks .logo_block").slideDown(600, "easeOutQuint");
                }
            }
            $.log(_content_logo_allocations);
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * L1 image crossfade plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["crossFade"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({
                selector: ">a>img:odd",
                duration: 400,
                //"interval" : 1330
                interval: 2666
            }, options);
            // ie fix
            if (!$.support.opacity) settings.interval *= 1.5;
            // main
            var $target = $(this).filter(":visible").find(settings.selector);
            var _timer = setInterval(function() {
                $target.stop(true, true).fadeToggle(settings.duration, "easeInOutQuart");
            }, settings.interval);
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    /*
     * animated page top plugin
     */
    (function($) {
        $.fn["animatedPageTop"] = function(options) {
            // settings
            var settings = $.extend({}, options);
            // main
            this.each(function() {
                $(this).click(function() {
                    //$(window).scrollTop(0);
                    $("html,body").animate({
                        scrollTop: 0
                    }, "slow", "easeOutQuart");
                    $(this).blur();
                    return false;
                });
            });
            return this;
        };
    })(jQuery);

    (function($) {
        // initialize
        $(function() {
            $(".imgover").rollover();
            $(".id_header").header();
            // lazy evaluation
            setTimeout(function() {
                $(".id_content_blocks>ul").logoAllocation();
                $(".id_content_blocks>ul>li").animatedRollover();
                $(".id_content_blocks .contentCrossFade").crossFade();
                $(".id_goPageTop>a").animatedPageTop();
            }, 600);
        });

    })(jQuery);
</script>

<script>
    var n = $(window).width();
    $(".box_boss").width(n).css({
        marginLeft: -n * 0.5
    });
    $(".box_show ul li img").width(n * ratio);
    var z = $(".box_subnav ul li").width();
    $(".box_subnav ul li").find("img").width(z);
    $(".box_subnav li").first().find(".current_img").show().css({
        marginTop: -10
    });
    var x = 0;
    $(".box_subnav ul li").click(function() {
        x = $(this).index();

        $(".box_run").stop().animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);

        $(this).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });
    $(".left_btn").click(function() {
        if (0 < x) {
            x = x - 1
        } else {
            x = $(".box_show ul li").length - 1
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });
    $(".right_btn").click(function() {
        if (x < $(".box_show ul li").length - 1) {
            x = x + 1
        } else {
            x = 0
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500)
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    });


    function run() {
        $(".box_run").stop(true, true);
        $(".current_img").stop(true, true);

        if (x < $(".box_show ul li").length - 1) {
            x = x + 1
        } else {
            x = 0
        };
        $(".box_run").animate({
            marginLeft: -n * ratio * x
        }, 500);
        $(".current_img").fadeOut().animate({
            marginTop: 40
        }, 200);
        $(".box_subnav li").eq(x).find(".current_img").fadeIn(50).animate({
            marginTop: -10
        }, 200);
    };
    /*setInterval(run,3000);*/
    t = setInterval(run, 3000);
    $(".box_show,.box_subnav ul li").mouseenter(function() {
        clearInterval(t)
    }).mouseleave(function() {
        //setInterval(run,3000)
        t = setInterval(run, 3000);
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var speed = 5e3;
        //�6������v�
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", 1);
        //��������
        /*���w*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").hover(function() {
            $(this).css({
                "background-position":"left bottom"
            });
        }, function() {
            $(this).removeAttr("style");
        });
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").click(function() {
            var page = $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data");
            ////
            var li_l = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w * 3;
            $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
            ////
            if (!$(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                //�6�|�y������������������
                if (page == li_l) {
                    //��m��
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li:first").clone().attr("id", "cop").appendTo($(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box"));
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                        width:ul_w + li_w + "px"
                    });
                    //��������
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            left:0
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            width:ul_w + "px"
                        });
                    });
                    page = 1;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                } else {
                    //����
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    });
                    page++;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                }
            }
        });
        /*���w����*/
        /*����w*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").hover(function() {
            $(this).css({
                "background-position":"left bottom"
            });
        }, function() {
            $(this).removeAttr("style");
        });
        $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").click(function() {
            var page = $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data");
            ////
            var li_l = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w;
            $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
            ////
            if (!$(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                if (page == 1) {
                    //��m��
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li:last").clone().attr("id", "cop").prependTo($(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box"));
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                        width:ul_w + li_w + "px",
                        left:-li_w
                    });
                    //�������<�����
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"+=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            left:-(li_w * (page - 1))
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                        $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").css({
                            width:ul_w + "px"
                        });
                    });
                    page = li_l;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                } else {
                    $(this).parent().find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"+=" + li_w
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                        $(this).parent().next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    });
                    page--;
                    $(this).prevAll("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                }
            }
        });
        /*����w����*/
        /*����|*/
        $("div.big_box_04 div.btn").each(function(i, n) {
            var a = $(n).width();
            var b = $(n).parent().width();
            /*$(n).css({left:(b/2)-(a/2)})*/
            $(n).find("div").each(function(j, m) {
                //���xa��������
                $(m).eq(j).css({
                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                });
                $(m).hover(function() {
                    if (!$(this).hasClass("this") && $(this).hasClass("bo")) {
                        $(this).css({
                            "background-position":"left bottom"
                        });
                    }
                }, function() {
                    if (!$(this).hasClass("this")) {
                        $(this).removeAttr("style");
                    }
                });
                ////
                var li_l = $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box li").width(), ul_w = li_l * li_w;
                $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
                ////
                $(m).mouseenter(function() {
                    $(this).addClass("this").css({
                        "background-position":"left bottom"
                    }).mouseleave(function() {
                        $(this).stop();
                    });
                    $(this).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                    $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").animate({
                        left:"-" + li_w * j
                    }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart");
                    page = j + 1;
                    //��������w
                    $(this).parent().prev("div.show_view").find("ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                });
            });
        });
        /*���=���*/
        /*�6����*/
        var boxliw = $(".big_box_04 .show_view").width();
        $("div.big_box_04").each(function(l, o) {
            var div_h = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box li img").height();
            var span_h = $(o).find("div.btn div").height();
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li").css("width", boxliw + "px");
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li img").css("width", boxliw + "px");
            $(o).find("ul.banner_box li img").css("height", "auto");
            /*$(o).css({height:div_h+span_h});
             $(o).find('div.show_view').css({height:div_h});*/
            var handle;
            function start_slide() {
                var page = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data");
                ////
                var li_l = $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box li[id!=cop]").length, li_w = boxliw, ul_w = li_l * li_w;
                $(o).find("ul.banner_box").css("width", ul_w + "px");
                ////
                handle = setInterval(function() {
                    if (!$(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").is(":animated")) {
                        //�6�|�y������������������
                        if (page == li_l) {
                            //��m��
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").find("li:first").clone().attr("id", "cop").appendTo($(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box"));
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").css({
                                width:ul_w + li_w + "px"
                            });
                            //��������
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").animate({
                                left:"-=" + li_w
                            }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                                $(this).css({
                                    left:0
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                                $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").find("li#cop").remove();
                                $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").css({
                                    width:ul_w + "px"
                                });
                            });
                            page = 1;
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                        } else {
                            //����
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").animate({
                                left:"-=" + li_w
                            }, "slow", "easeInOutQuart", function() {
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).addClass("this").css({
                                    "background-position":"left bottom"
                                });
                                $(o).find("div.show_view").next("div.btn").find("div").eq(page - 1).siblings().removeClass("this").removeAttr("style");
                            });
                            page++;
                            $(o).find("div.show_view ul.banner_box").data("data", page);
                        }
                    }
                }, speed);
            }
            ///
            function stop_slide() {
                clearInterval(handle);
            }
            //////
            setTimeout(function() {
                start_slide();
            }, 0);
            //����IEbug
            $(o).hover(function() {
                //�6����
                stop_slide();
            }, function() {
                start_slide();
            });
        });
    });

    $(window).bind("load", function() {

            $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view ul.banner_box li").removeAttr("style");

    $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.right").hide();

    $("div.big_box_04 div.show_view div.left").hide();

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
        var categoryPage = false;
        $('.id_navHeader>li>a[class^="id_header_"]').click(function () {
            categoryPage = true;
            var target = $(this).attr('href').substr(2);
            $("div.navSubSectionHeader").hide();
            $("div.navPlaceholder").hide();
            $("div.navPlaceholder_" + target).show();
            $('div.navSubSectionHeader_' + target).show();
        });
        $("area.navSectionHeader").click(function () {
            if (categoryPage) {
                var ref = $(this).attr('data-ref');
                $(".id_navHeader>li>a[href='" + ref + "']").trigger('click');
                return false;
            }
        });
        $("a.id_top").click(function () {
            categoryPage = false;
            $("div.navSubSectionHeader").show();
            $("div.navPlaceholder").show();
        });
    });
</script>
